normalizedQuery: string,\n214\t  originalQuery: string\n215\t): boolean {\n216\t  const normalizedName = normalizeForSearch(station.name);\n217\t  const expandedQuery = normalizedName.includes(normalizedQuery) ||\n222\t    normalizedName.includes(expandedQuery) ||\n223\t    normalizedName.includes(expandedNormalizedQuery)\n224\t  ) {\n225\t    return true;\n226\t  }\n227\t\n228\t  const upperQuery = originalQuery.toUpperCase();\n229\t  if (station.lines.some((line) => line === upperQuery)) {\n230\t    return true;\n231\t  }\n232\t\n233\t  const expandedName = 1;\n264\t}\n265\t\n266\tfunction buildStationToComplexMap(complexes: ComplexIndex): Map<string, StationComplex> {\n267\t  const map = new Map<string, StationComplex>();\n268\t  for (const complex of Supports brotli, gzip, and deflate based on Accept-Encoding header.\n289\t * Brotli is preferred for best compression ratio.\n290\t */\n291\tfunction compressionMiddleware(): MiddlewareHandler {\n292\t  return async (c, next) => {\n293\t    await next();\n294\t\n295\t    const body = c.res.body;\n296\t    if (!body || c.res.headers.get(\"Content-Encoding\")) return;\n297\t\n298\t    const contentType = c.res.headers.get(\"Content-Type\");\n299\t    if (!contentType?.includes(\"json\") && !contentType?.includes(\"text\")) return;\n300\t\n301\t    const acceptEncoding = c.req.header(\"Accept-Encoding\") || \"\";\n302\t    const contentLength = c.res.headers.get(\"Content-Length\");\n303\t\n304\t    // Skip small responses (not worth compressing)\n305\t    if (contentLength && parseInt(contentLength, 10) < 500) return;\n306\t\n307\t    // Clone response to get the body as buffer\n308\t    const buffer = Buffer.from(await c.res.clone().arrayBuffer());\n309\t\n310\t    // Prefer brotli for best compression, then gzip, then deflate\n311\t    if (acceptEncoding.includes(\"br\")) {\n312\t      const brotlied = await new Promise<Buffer>((resolve, reject) => {\n313\t        const chunks: Buffer[] = [];\n314\t        const brotli = createBrotliCompress();\n315\t        brotli.on(\"data\", (chunk) => chunks.push(chunk));\n316\t        brotli.on(\"end\", () => resolve(Buffer.concat(chunks)));\n317\t        brotli.on(\"error\", reject);\n318\t        brotli.end(buffer);\n319\t      });\n320\t\n321\t      c.res = new Response(brotlied, {\n322\t        status: c.res.status,\n323\t        headers: c.res.headers,\n324\t      });\n325\t      c.res.headers.set(\"Content-Encoding\", \"br\");\n326\t      c.res.headers.delete(\"Content-Length\");\n327\t    } else if (acceptEncoding.includes(\"gzip\")) {\n328\t      const gzipped = await new Promise<Buffer>((resolve, reject) => {\n329\t        const chunks: Buffer[] = [];\n330\t        const gzip = createGzip();\n331\t        gzip.on(\"data\", (chunk) => chunks.push(chunk));\n332\t        gzip.on(\"end\", () => resolve(Buffer.concat(chunks)));\n333\t        gzip.on(\"error\", reject);\n334\t        gzip.end(buffer);\n335\t      });\n336\t\n337\t      c.res = new Response(gzipped, {\n338\t        status: c.res.status,\n339\t        headers: c.res.headers,\n340\t      });\n341\t      c.res.headers.set(\"Content-Encoding\", \"gzip\");\n342\t      c.res.headers.delete(\"Content-Length\");\n343\t    } else if (acceptEncoding.includes(\"deflate\")) {\n344\t      const deflated = await new Promise<Buffer>((resolve, reject) => {\n345\t        const chunks: Buffer[] = [];\n346\t        const deflate = createDeflate();\n347\t        deflate.on(\"data\", (chunk) => chunks.push(chunk));\n348\t        deflate.on(\"end\", () => resolve(Buffer.concat(chunks)));\n349\t        deflate.on(\"error\", reject);\n350\t        deflate.end(buffer);\n351\t      });\n352\t\n353\t      c.res = new Response(deflated, {\n354\t        status: c.res.status,\n355\t        headers: c.res.headers,\n356\t      });\n357\t      c.res.headers.set(\"Content-Encoding\", \"deflate\");\n358\t      c.res.headers.delete(\"Content-Length\");\n359\t    }\n360\t  };\n361\t}\n362\t\n363\t/**\n364\t * Check if a path has
